Top 32 Decklists
================



 Posted in **Event Coverage**
 on August 14, 2016 






![](https://media.magic.wizards.com/styles/auth_small/public/images/person/authorpic_FrankKarsten.jpg)
By Frank Karsten











There is more to this event than just the Top 8. Below are the decklists of the players who finished in 9th through 32nd place. Although the Top 8 featured only Bant Company and U/R Fevered Burn, the Top 32 has a variety of decks featuring [Liliana, the Last Hope](http://gatherer.wizards.com/Pages/Card/Details.aspx?name=Liliana%2C+the+Last+Hope), [Emrakul, the Promised End](http://gatherer.wizards.com/Pages/Card/Details.aspx?name=Emrakul%2C+the+Promised+End), [Elder Deep-Fiend](http://gatherer.wizards.com/Pages/Card/Details.aspx?name=Elder+Deep-Fiend), and/or more.







#### Fredrik Joelsson's Temur Emerge – 9th at Grand Prix Rimini 2016


##### 






![](https://web.archive.org/web/20160726232508im_/http://magic.wizards.com/sites/all/modules/features/wiz_bean_content_deck_list/icons/decklist_download.png)
